sides.

Custom side textures for farmland.

Added some thickness to the vines.

Subtle change to the sides of the fence gates.

Adjusted the Tinted Glass border.

Animated Enderpearl.

Warped and Crimson Hyphae were not using the correct top and bottom textures.

OptiFine custom colours fully updated to the new 384 world heights.

Double the resolution for the lightmaps for the Overworld, Nether and The End.

Recalculated the Sheep, Wolf Collar and Dye custom colours.

New fuzzy edge overlay for dirt, this makes the river beds look a lot better when there is clay or
stone next to dirt blocks.

Added cullface on glass pane edges.

Cleaned up all the OptiFine CTM properties files so all the settings are now specified for each
block, with OptiFine if settings are missing OptiFine will just use it's default setting, this did
not work too well with the Nuclearfarts 'connected-block-textures' fabric mod.

Sugar Cane, Logs and Stems (including stripped logs and stems) CTM doesn't work correctly.

Overlay do not currently work at all in the connected-block-textures fabric mod.

Wrong end texture on horizontal Crimson Stem blocks, thanks to TechZerker on Discord for pointing it
out.

Flipped the texture on one side of the stonecutter so the blade looks correct on both sides now.

Fixed the Minecart texture, has always had some textures flipped upsidedown.

Adjusted the Grindstone texture mapping.

Added cross pattern to the Black Wool, cleaned up some missing pixels on the other wools.

Black Enderman bed.

Moved the Sunflower head so there less of a gap to the stem, also adjusted the stem.

Fixed the Wolf rear texture that's always been upsidedown, also made the collar bigger.

More font fun to be had, the font files are getting too large to work with a will not work on some
systems due to the large sizes (one wwas 14400px tall!!!), I've had to half texture size for the
three font files, quality is still good as it's still four times vanilla size.

Still quite a few fonts not textured.

Cleaned up the tiling for Crimson and Warped Nylium.

Adjusted the colours for all the warped blocks to make them a little more vibrant.

Less blurred Honeycomb and Wart Blocks.

Two tusks Hoglin-Piglin and two legs Strider.

Added some noise to the Phantoms.

Fixed the position of the Piglin and Zombified Piglin gold earrings, also changed the left and right
arms & legs as you can now have them be different textures.

-21st February 2020 - Minecraft 20w08a--------------------------------------------------------------

Defaulted to the true type font to see if the pack still crashes on load.

If your game crashes when loading the pack rename some files.

Rename default.json to default1.json and rename default2.json to default.json.

/assets/minecraft/font/default.json
/assets/minecraft/font/default2.json

This will make the resource pack use the bitmap font instead.

A few more Villagers completed, only two to go.

I'm making them all different so you will know a villagers profession without talking to them.

eg.

The farmer wears green wellington boots, has a sprew of wheat in his mouth, a wicker hat and large
side burns.

Weaponsmith has an eye patch as he clearly was not wearing his eye protection when working unlike
his colleague, the Toolsmith who follows the rules.

Butcher wears a dirty white apron with blood on it where he was butchering some animal.

Leatherworkers apparel is pretty much all brown leather with a brown leather cap.

Stonecutter gui.

-26th July 2018 - Minecraft 1.13.0 v2---------------------------------------------------------------

This pack now uses a bitmapped font by default, if you want sharper, better looking text and have a
powerful computer you may wnat to use the new True Type Font but Minecraft may crash on older less
powerful hardware, just rename the "default1.json" to "default.json" in the font directory and
reload the resource pack.

                textures/items/spectral_arrow.png.mcmeta
                textures/items/tropical_fish_bucket.png.mcmeta
                textures/items/water_bucket.png.mcmeta

Cullface all faces, why drawn a face when you cannot see it, very minute performance gain.

Tweaked the Salmon fin colours.

Cod and Salmon.

The mcmeta is more strict with it's formatting, there were some extra commas on the last frame of
some of them which stopped some animated textures loading.

Tweaked the font resolution, I always wanted the best quality for the text but I forgot that other
players may be playing on older hardward or laptops.

They were 256px per character which made the accented.png 4604x6912, which is stupidly large and may
have been the thing causing the crashes when trying to load the resource pack, I tried 64px but they
look notically bad compaired to the ttf.

So I've dropped them in half at no noticeable change in quality, so the font is now 128px per
character, this will hopefully sort out the crashing issue when trying to create the textures-atlas.

When Minecraft loads a resource pack it creates a texture-atlas, this is a single image file
containing every texture in the pack including all the fonts, frames from an animated texture like
water, as more stuff is added to the pack this file gets bigger and eventually you can run out of
RAM, you would see this a lot more on the larger resource pack (64x, 128x etc...), this is why some
packs need a higher spec PC.

Anyway I've made the ttf optional and only use the bitmapped font now.

The True Type Fonts do look sharper but if the game cannot be played it's not much use, maybe I'll
have the ttf fonts as an option for people with more powerful systems.

pack, I tried adding Berylium font, while it does work it's missing all the European characters as

basically it looks like crap.

Hopefully bitmap font will come back as it does give you more choice.

Almost all the blockstates and models had to be edited to use the newer texture names and also the
newer, simpler way of doing certain things like slabs, fences, gates, pistons and lots more.

-{v1.4.0}- 29th February 2016 - Minecraft 1.9.0-----------------------------------------------------

Here we go; Minecraft 1.9.0 is out and is now the current release in the launcher.

Over the last month or so I've been going through the pack, cleaning up, making lots of consistency
and quality improvements.

I decided to add some custom models without them standing out too much and being too obvious in the
game, things like the Ladder now has some depth, Trapdoors and Doors now have edges too, more to
come in the future.

Some hand held items were rendered using flat 2D sprites but have internal 3D models when placed on
the ground, so why not use the model that already exists in the game, so items like the Brewing
Stand, Cauldron, Comparator, Flower Pot, Hopper, Repeater and Tripwire Hook now all use the 3D
models when held in the hand, on your head, on the ground or in your inventory.

There've been hundreds of changes to the pack to make it compatible with 1.9.0 and lots of tweaks
and additions, see the full changelog below for all the details and go play some Minecraft.

JimStoneCraft

-{15w40b}- 3rd October 2015 - 1.9 - 15w40b----------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<UPDATED>
                font/glyph_sizes.bin
                textures/font/ascii.png
                textures/font/unicode_page_00.png
                textures/font/unicode_page_01.png
                textures/entity/horse/horse_skeleton.png

Tweaked all the fonts, also finally added the very hard to edit glyph_sizes.bin, this file is used
by Minecraft for the unicode character widths (kerning).

Note that the glyph_sizes.bin in only loaded when Minecraft loads, so you have to load Minecraft,
select the Resource Pack, exit Minecraft and then reload Minecraft, you only have to do this if
you need to use the Force Unicode Font option, this is a work around to a known Minecraft bug but at
least it works for now.

https://bugs.mojang.com/browse/MC-41270

The unicode_page_00 and unicode_page_01 fonts cover most of the diacritic marks used in the 
language regions like Germanic, Celtic, Romance, Slavic, Baltic, Finno-Ugric, Turkic and others.

Hopefully this will be good news to all the non English speaking players that use the John Smith
Legacy Resource Pack but were previously forced to use the English font only.

When I added the horses I was a little lazy, as the skeleton horse was not used I never made a
texture for it, that's now been rectified, I've not done the Zombie horse yet as that's not in the
vanilla game yet but I'm sure that will change.

Added the unicode_page_01.png, One issue though is the unicode fonts are fixed width (no

width fonts to the unicode files like they did with the standard ascii fonts.

-{1.3.14}- 30th April 2015 - 1.8.4------------------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<UPDATED>
                mcpatcher/ctm/stained_glass_light_blue.properties
                mcpatcher/ctm/stained_glass_pane_light_blue.properties
                mcpatcher/ctm/stained_glass_silver.properties
                mcpatcher/ctm/stained_glass_pane_silver.properties

lightBlue vs light_blue, MCPatcher vs Optifine.

You have to love the inconsistencies in the game that is Minecraft, while lightBlue is the in game
name, MCPatcher uses light_blue while Optifine uses lightBlue, I follow the MCPatcher standard.

Also the Stained Glass Panes ctm doesn't currently display correctly in MCPatcher or Optifine,
Optifine shows the black and pink chequerboard on the inside surfaces while MCPatcher shows just
the standard panes (not joined).

EDIT: Changed the matchBlocks so it works in both MCPatcher vs Optifine.

The "minecraft:" prefix is optional with MCPatcher but looks like Optifine requires it, I've added
it for the silver glass and is in this release.

Here's a quote from the MCPatcher help files, looks like Optifine requires the full name.

# In 1.7, blocks are referred to by name rather than number.  Numerical IDs are
# supported for older blocks, but newer blocks will be name only.  Stone blocks
# for example can be referred to as
#   1               (not recommended)
#   minecraft:stone (full name)
#   stone           (name without prefix)

Thanks to Roman0 in the forums for the bug report.



-{1.3.13}- 19th April 2015 - 1.8.4------------------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<UPDATED>
                textures/blocks/cauldron_bottom.png
                textures/blocks/cauldron_inner.png
                textures/blocks/cauldron_side.png

JimStoneCraft
<ADDED>
                models/block/cauldron_empty.json
                models/block/cauldron_level1.json
                models/block/cauldron_level2.json
                models/block/cauldron_level3.json
                textures/blocks/cauldron_inner_side.png

Fixed a Mojang Cauldron bug that would "cullface" the bottom face, still not fixed in the actual
game though as the bug tracker can be a little slow, please go and upvote the fix.

https://bugs.mojang.com/browse/MC-58405

Also the way Minecraft draws the Cauldron and the Minecraft anti X-Ray block transparency feature,
the Cauldron used to be just the textures listed below displayed for the various sides:-

cauldron_bottom.png
cauldron_inner.png
cauldron_side.png
cauldron_top.png

But now the Cauldron is a model (like the Anvil), which means the legs are now drawn on the inside
too, as the John Smith textures had more slender legs you now get get the white pixels when using
the JSL textures (from the Minecraft anti X-Ray "feature").

The two options are draw the leg textures bigger to suit the default model or make the model file
suit the JSL textures.

I decided to go with the first option as it's a little easier to do but then with some testing found
quite a few issue in the way the textures are drawn on the vanilla Cauldron (stretching and
rotation issues).

After that I then decided to make my own model to better suit the JSL textures (with the slender
legs), with more testing I've also added a custom bottom and inside texture.

Thanks to Alpha_Wolf777 in the forums for the bug report.

WIP for the new random textures using blockstates and models, most of the textures are done but I do
have a few of the more complex configs to do.

With the new system you can now have bottom faces for blocks that never had bottom faces before.

Furnace, Dispenser, Dropper and Crafting Table still need to be made.

The old Book Shelf just used the Oak Plank texture for the top and bottom, it now has it's own
custom top and bottom texture.

The bed used the Oak Planks texture for the bottom of the bed, it now has a custom texture.

blockstates I've got random textures working for Oak Planks, as the new system is not quite final
yet I'll leave it at that for now.

-{1.2.18}- 23rd May 2014 - 1.7.9--------------------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<UPDATED>
[JimStoneCraft] textures/particle/particle.png
                textures/blocks/fire_layer_0.png
                textures/blocks/fire_layer_1.png
                textures/blocks/torch_on.png

New flame effect when using a furnace or a torch in the same style as the fire layer, the smoke and
flames are now 60% transparent.

Adjusted the potion swirls to make them thinner and more round, arrow firing also made thinner, both
are now 40% tranparent to make them less intrusive.

Water bubble and rain bounce drops also 40% tranparent.

Partially transparent pixels cannot be on the fire layer or torch blocks, pixels with 50% or less
transparency are just removed by Minecraft and pixels with 51% or more transparency are just made
solid, so I cleaned up the textures as they had transparent pixels that didn't show up anyway.

                textures/font/ascii.properties
                textures/font/unicode_page_00.properties

Cleaned up the Spruce Opaque leaves.

Made the Map Icons much clearer (32x32px for each icon now).

Cleaned up the top and bottom CTM properties for the monster spawners as there were some errors.

Tweaked the Potatos to be a little rounder.

I had no plans on testing this pack in Optifine but decided to do some limited testing anyway as
some people are having some issues.

In Minecraft 1.7 onwards, blocks are referred to by name rather than ID number.

Numerical IDs are supported for older blocks currently, but newer blocks will be name only. 
 
Stone blocks for example can be referred to as:-
   1               (not recommended)
   minecraft:stone (full name)
   stone           (name without prefix)
   
The trouble is Optifine still uses ID's so this is why the custom colours are not working correctly.

I've temporarily change the names back to ID's (names are still in the color.properties files but
are commented out) as at least this is currently compatible with both Optifine and MCPatcher but
with new blocks coming along like Granite, these will not even have an ID number and go by just a
name so this will have to change to the newer system in the end anyway.

Some things like the trip wire hooks and lever do not work in Optifine (they will look default).

As the font can display wrong with Optifine, I've removed the two font kerning properties files.

-{1.2.1}- 28th October 2013 - 1.7.2-----------------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<UPDATED>
[JimStoneCraft] textures/entity/spider_eyes.png
                mcpatcher/color.properties

It would seem to be that the spider_eyes.png file doesn't need an alpha transparent background, when
you just have black it works fine.

I don't use Custom Colors myself (Custom Colors off in MCPatcher) as I like the look of the original
colours in Minecraft, but I though I would investigate the grey grass issue anyway.

Minecraft has been slowly adding features that MCPatcher use to only have, this included custom
colours for biomes, grass, swampfoliage etc...

The color.properties file was a little out of date, this would cause the grass to turn grey when
patched as it was trying to add a tint to the grass, instead it would override the colour
completely, all working now.

-{1.1.13}- 18th October 2013 - 13w42b---------------------------------------------------------------

JimStoneCraft
<ADDED>
[JimStoneCraft] textures/blocks/glass_white.png
                textures/blocks/glass_silver.png
                textures/blocks/glass_pane_top_white
                textures/blocks/glass_pane_top_silver

These two textures are / (Japanese Fusuma/shji) style sliding panels.

The glass_silver.png texture is based on one of the alternative John Smith Glow
Stone textures, both glass_pane_top_white and glass_pane_top_silver have edges
that match the panes.

The glass_silver.png is 10% transparent and glass_white.png is 5% transparent, this is so it lets
light through for a great nighttime effect, plus the paper panels would let light through in real
life but would not be see through.

-{1.1.0}- (Complete Texture pack conversion to Resource Pack for 1.6)-------------------------------

Greenhawk837:
<UPDATED>
-Texture pack conversion to Resource Pack for 1.6 by JimStoneCraft
This pack is no longer backwards compatible
MCPatcher 4.1.0-beta3 (or greater) is required for HD font, random mobs, better skies etc...

<ADDED>
JimStoneCraft's READ ME
JimStoneCraft's Updated 512px Font (128px version is still there if needed)

NOTE:- Minecraft changed the way Texture packs are layed out and renamed them Resource Packs, this
pack is no longer backwards compatible and will not work with versions of Minecraft older than 1.6.

Please download the older Texture Pack for 1.52 and 1.47 compatibility.

http://www.jslegacy.com/
